    45	            "json" => Ok(Self::Json),
    46	            "default" => Ok(Self::Default),
    47	            "unix" => Ok(Self::Unix),
    48	            "checkstyle" => Ok(Self::Checkstyle),

    73	/// The Formatter is then managed by [`OutputFormatter`].
    74	trait InternalFormatter {
    75	    /// Print all available rules by oxlint
    76	    fn all_rules(&self, _enabled_rules: FxHashSet<&str>) -> Option<String> {
    77	        None
    78	    }
    79

    81	    fn lint_command_info(&self, _lint_command_info: &LintCommandInfo) -> Option<String> {
    82	        None
    83	    }
    84	
    85	    /// oxlint words with [`DiagnosticService`](oxc_diagnostics::DiagnosticService),
    86	    /// which uses a own reporter to output to stdout.
    87	    fn get_diagnostic_reporter(&self) -> Box<dyn DiagnosticReporter>;
    88	}

    90	pub struct OutputFormatter {
    91	    internal: Box<dyn InternalFormatter>,
    92	}
    93	
    94	impl OutputFormatter {
    95	    pub fn new(format: OutputFormat) -> Self {
    96	        Self { internal: Self::get_internal_formatter(format) }
    97	    }
    98	
    99	    fn get_internal_formatter(format: OutputFormat) -> Box<dyn InternalFormatter> {
   100	        match format {
   101	            OutputFormat::Json => Box::<JsonOutputFormatter>::default(),
   102	            OutputFormat::Checkstyle => Box::<CheckStyleOutputFormatter>::default(),
   103	            OutputFormat::Github => Box::new(GithubOutputFormatter),
   104	            OutputFormat::Gitlab => Box::<GitlabOutputFormatter>::default(),
   105	            OutputFormat::Unix => Box::<UnixOutputFormatter>::default(),
   106	            OutputFormat::Default => Box::new(DefaultOutputFormatter),
   107	            OutputFormat::Stylish => Box::<StylishOutputFormatter>::default(),
   108	            OutputFormat::JUnit => Box::<JUnitOutputFormatter>::default(),
   109	        }
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    /// Print all available rules by oxlint
   113	    /// See [`InternalFormatter::all_rules`] for more details.
   114	    pub fn all_rules(&self, enabled_rules: FxHashSet<&str>) -> Option<String> {
   115	        self.internal.all_rules(enabled_rules)
   116	    }
   117	
   118	    /// At the end of the Lint command we may output extra information.
   119	    pub fn lint_command_info(&self, lint_command_info: &LintCommandInfo) -> Option<String> {
   120	        self.internal.lint_command_info(lint_command_info)
   121	    }
   122	
   123	    /// Returns the [`DiagnosticReporter`] which then will be used by [`DiagnosticService`](oxc_diagnostics::DiagnosticService)
   124	    /// See [`InternalFormatter::get_diagnostic_reporter`] for more details.
   125	    pub fn get_diagnostic_reporter(&self) -> Box<dyn DiagnosticReporter> {
   126	        self.internal.get_diagnostic_reporter()
   127	    }

     2	
     3	use crate::output_formatter::InternalFormatter;
     4	use oxc_diagnostics::{
     5	    Error, GraphicalReportHandler,
     6	    reporter::{DiagnosticReporter, DiagnosticResult},
     7	};
     8	use oxc_linter::table::RuleTable;

    10	
    11	#[derive(Debug)]
    12	pub struct DefaultOutputFormatter;
    13	
    14	impl InternalFormatter for DefaultOutputFormatter {
    15	    fn all_rules(&self, enabled_rules: FxHashSet<&str>) -> Option<String> {
    16	        let mut output = String::new();
    17	        let table = RuleTable::default();
    18	        for section in &table.sections {
    19	            output.push_str(&section.render_markdown_table_cli(&enabled_rules));
    20	            output.push('\n');
    21	        }
    22	        output.push_str(format!("Default: {}\n", table.turned_on_by_default_count).as_str());
    23	        output.push_str(format!("Total: {}\n", table.total).as_str());
    24	        Some(output)
    25	    }
    26	
    27	    fn lint_command_info(&self, lint_command_info: &super::LintCommandInfo) -> Option<String> {
    28	        let time = Self::get_execution_time(&lint_command_info.start_time);
    29	        let s = if lint_command_info.number_of_files == 1 { "" } else { "s" };
    30	
    31	        if let Some(number_of_rules) = lint_command_info.number_of_rules {
    32	            Some(format!(
    33	                "Finished in {time} on {} file{s} with {} rules using {} threads.\n",
    34	                lint_command_info.number_of_files, number_of_rules, lint_command_info.threads_count
    35	            ))
    36	        } else {
    37	            Some(format!(
    38	                "Finished in {time} on {} file{s} using {} threads.\n",
    39	                lint_command_info.number_of_files, lint_command_info.threads_count
    40	            ))
    41	        }
    42	    }
    43	
    44	    #[cfg(not(any(test, feature = "testing")))]
    45	    fn get_diagnostic_reporter(&self) -> Box<dyn DiagnosticReporter> {
    46	        Box::new(GraphicalReporter::default())
    47	    }

    54	    }

    57	impl DefaultOutputFormatter {
    58	    fn get_execution_time(duration: &Duration) -> String {
    59	        let ms = duration.as_millis();
    60	        if ms < 1000 { format!("{ms}ms") } else { format!("{:.1}s", duration.as_secs_f64()) }
    61	    }
    62	}

    64	/// Pretty-prints diagnostics. Primarily meant for human-readable output in a terminal.
    65	///
    66	/// See [`GraphicalReportHandler`] for how to configure colors, context lines, etc.
    67	#[cfg_attr(all(not(test), feature = "testing"), expect(dead_code))]
    68	struct GraphicalReporter {
    69	    handler: GraphicalReportHandler,
    70	}
    71	
    72	impl Default for GraphicalReporter {
    73	    fn default() -> Self {
    74	        Self { handler: GraphicalReportHandler::new() }
    75	    }
    76	}
    77	
    78	impl DiagnosticReporter for GraphicalReporter {
    79	    fn finish(&mut self, result: &DiagnosticResult) -> Option<String> {
    80	        Some(get_diagnostic_result_output(result))
    81	    }
    82	
    83	    fn render_error(&mut self, error: Error) -> Option<String> {
    84	        let mut output = String::new();
    85	        self.handler.render_report(&mut output, error.as_ref()).unwrap();
    86	        Some(output)
    87	    }
    88	}
    89	
    90	pub(super) fn get_diagnostic_result_output(result: &DiagnosticResult) -> String {
    91	    let mut output = String::new();
    92	
    93	    if result.warnings_count() + result.errors_count() > 0 {
    94	        output.push('\n');
    95	    }
    96	
    97	    output.push_str(
    98	        format!(
    99	            "Found {} warning{} and {} error{}.\n",
   100	            result.warnings_count(),
   101	            if result.warnings_count() == 1 { "" } else { "s" },
   102	            result.errors_count(),
   103	            if result.errors_count() == 1 { "" } else { "s" },
   104	        )
   105	        .as_str(),
   106	    );
   107	
   108	    if result.max_warnings_exceeded() {
   109	        output.push_str(
   110	            format!("Exceeded maximum number of warnings. Found {}.\n", result.warnings_count())
   111	                .as_str(),
   112	        );
   113	    }
   114	
   115	    output
   116	}

   119	mod test_implementation {
   120	    use oxc_diagnostics::{
   121	        Error, GraphicalReportHandler, GraphicalTheme,
   122	        reporter::{DiagnosticReporter, DiagnosticResult, Info},
   123	    };
   124	
   125	    use crate::output_formatter::default::get_diagnostic_result_output;
   126	
   127	    #[derive(Default)]
   128	    pub struct GraphicalReporterTester {
   129	        diagnostics: Vec<Error>,
   130	    }
   131	
   132	    impl DiagnosticReporter for GraphicalReporterTester {
   133	        fn finish(&mut self, result: &DiagnosticResult) -> Option<String> {
   134	            let handler = GraphicalReportHandler::new_themed(GraphicalTheme::none())
   135	                // links print ansi escape codes, which makes snapshots harder to read
   136	                .with_links(false);
   137	            let mut output = String::new();
   138	
   139	            self.diagnostics.sort_by_cached_key(|diagnostic| {
   140	                let info = Info::new(diagnostic);
   141	                (info.filename, info.start, info.end, info.rule_id, info.message)
   142	            });
   143	
   144	            for diagnostic in &self.diagnostics {
   145	                handler.render_report(&mut output, diagnostic.as_ref()).unwrap();
   146	            }
   147	
   148	            output.push_str(&get_diagnostic_result_output(result));
   149	
   150	            Some(output)

    10	
    11	#[derive(Debug)]
    12	pub struct GithubOutputFormatter;
    13	
    14	impl InternalFormatter for GithubOutputFormatter {
    15	    fn get_diagnostic_reporter(&self) -> Box<dyn DiagnosticReporter> {
    16	        Box::new(GithubReporter)

    19	
    20	/// Formats reports using [GitHub Actions
    21	/// annotations](https://docs.github.com/en/actions/reference/workflow-commands-for-github-actions#setting-an-error-message). Useful for reporting in CI.
    22	struct GithubReporter;
    23	
    24	impl DiagnosticReporter for GithubReporter {
    25	    fn finish(&mut self, result: &DiagnosticResult) -> Option<String> {
    26	        Some(get_diagnostic_result_output(result))
    27	    }
    28	
    29	    fn supports_minified_file_fallback(&self) -> bool {
    30	        false
    31	    }
    32	
    33	    fn render_error(&mut self, error: Error) -> Option<String> {
    34	        Some(format_github(&error))
    35	    }
    36	}
    37	
    38	fn format_github(diagnostic: &Error) -> String {
    39	    let Info { start, end, filename, message, severity, rule_id } = Info::new(diagnostic);
    40	    let severity = match severity {
    41	        Severity::Error => "error",
    42	        Severity::Warning | miette::Severity::Advice => "warning",
    43	    };
    44	    let title = rule_id.map_or(Cow::Borrowed("oxlint"), Cow::Owned);
    45	    let filename = escape_property(&filename);
    46	    let message = escape_data(&message);
    47	    format!(
    48	        "::{severity} file={filename},line={},endLine={},col={},endColumn={},title={title}::{message}\n",
    49	        start.line, end.line, start.column, end.column
    50	    )
    51	}
    52	
    53	fn escape_data(value: &str) -> String {
    54	    // Refs:
    55	    // - https://github.com/actions/runner/blob/a4c57f27477077e57545af79851551ff7f5632bd/src/Runner.Common/ActionCommand.cs#L18-L22
    56	    // - https://github.com/actions/toolkit/blob/fe3e7ce9a7f995d29d1fcfd226a32bca407f9dc8/packages/core/src/command.ts#L80-L94
    57	    let mut result = String::with_capacity(value.len());
    58	    for c in value.chars() {
    59	        match c {
    60	            '\r' => result.push_str("%0D"),
    61	            '\n' => result.push_str("%0A"),
    62	            '%' => result.push_str("%25"),
    63	            _ => result.push(c),
    64	        }
    65	    }
    66	    result
    67	}
    68	
    69	fn escape_property(value: &str) -> String {
    70	    // Refs:
    71	    // - https://github.com/actions/runner/blob/a4c57f27477077e57545af79851551ff7f5632bd/src/Runner.Common/ActionCommand.cs#L25-L32
    72	    // - https://github.com/actions/toolkit/blob/fe3e7ce9a7f995d29d1fcfd226a32bca407f9dc8/packages/core/src/command.ts#L80-L94
    73	    let mut result = String::with_capacity(value.len());
    74	    for c in value.chars() {
    75	        match c {
    76	            '\r' => result.push_str("%0D"),
    77	            '\n' => result.push_str("%0A"),
    78	            ':' => result.push_str("%3A"),
    79	            ',' => result.push_str("%2C"),
    80	            '%' => result.push_str("%25"),
    81	            _ => result.push(c),
    82	        }
    83	    }
    84	    result
    85	}

   128	
   129	/// NAPI entry point.
   130	///
   131	/// JS side passes in:
   132	/// 1. `args`: Command line arguments (process.argv.slice(2))
   133	/// 2. `load_plugin`: Load a JS plugin from a file path.
   134	/// 3. `setup_rule_configs`: Setup configuration options.
   135	/// 4. `lint_file`: Lint a file.
   136	/// 5. `create_workspace`: Create a workspace.
   137	/// 6. `destroy_workspace`: Destroy a workspace.
   138	/// 7. `load_js_configs`: Load JavaScript config files.
   139	///
   140	/// Returns `true` if linting succeeded without errors, `false` otherwise.
   141	#[expect(clippy::allow_attributes)]
   142	#[allow(clippy::trailing_empty_array, clippy::unused_async)] // https://github.com/napi-rs/napi-rs/issues/2758
   143	#[napi]
   144	pub async fn lint(
   145	    args: Vec<String>,
   146	    load_plugin: JsLoadPluginCb,
   147	    setup_rule_configs: JsSetupRuleConfigsCb,
   148	    lint_file: JsLintFileCb,
   149	    create_workspace: JsCreateWorkspaceCb,
   150	    destroy_workspace: JsDestroyWorkspaceCb,
   151	    load_js_configs: JsLoadJsConfigsCb,
   152	) -> bool {
   153	    lint_impl(
   154	        args,
   155	        load_plugin,
   156	        setup_rule_configs,
   157	        lint_file,
   158	        create_workspace,
   159	        destroy_workspace,
   160	        load_js_configs,
   161	    )
   162	    .await
   163	    .report()
   164	        == ExitCode::SUCCESS
   165	}
   166	
   167	/// Run the linter.
   168	async fn lint_impl(
   169	    args: Vec<String>,
   170	    load_plugin: JsLoadPluginCb,
   171	    setup_rule_configs: JsSetupRuleConfigsCb,
   172	    lint_file: JsLintFileCb,
   173	    create_workspace: JsCreateWorkspaceCb,
   174	    destroy_workspace: JsDestroyWorkspaceCb,
   175	    load_js_configs: JsLoadJsConfigsCb,
   176	) -> CliRunResult {
   177	    // Convert String args to OsString for compatibility with bpaf
   178	    let args: Vec<std::ffi::OsString> = args.into_iter().map(std::ffi::OsString::from).collect();
   179	
   180	    let command = {
   181	        let cmd = crate::cli::lint_command();
   182	        match cmd.run_inner(&*args) {
   183	            Ok(cmd) => cmd,
   184	            Err(e) => {
   185	                e.print_message(100);
   186	                return if e.exit_code() == 0 {
   187	                    CliRunResult::LintSucceeded
   188	                } else {
   189	                    CliRunResult::InvalidOptionConfig
   190	                };
   191	            }
   192	        }
   193	    };
   194	
   195	    // Both LSP and CLI use `tracing` for logging
   196	    init_tracing();
   197	
   198	    // JS plugins are only supported on 64-bit little-endian platforms at present
   199	    #[cfg(all(target_pointer_width = "64", target_endian = "little"))]
   200	    let (external_linter, js_config_loader) = {
   201	        let js_config_loader = Some(crate::js_config::create_js_config_loader(load_js_configs));
   202	        let external_linter = Some(crate::js_plugins::create_external_linter(
   203	            load_plugin,
   204	            setup_rule_configs,
   205	            lint_file,
   206	            create_workspace,
   207	            destroy_workspace,
   208	        ));
   209	        (external_linter, js_config_loader)
   210	    };
   211	    #[cfg(not(all(target_pointer_width = "64", target_endian = "little")))]
   212	    let (external_linter, js_config_loader) = {
   213	        let (_, _, _, _, _, _) = (
   214	            load_plugin,
   215	            setup_rule_configs,
   216	            lint_file,
   217	            create_workspace,
   218	            destroy_workspace,
   219	            load_js_configs,
   220	        );
   221	        (None, None)
   222	    };
   223	
   224	    // If --lsp flag is set, run the language server
   225	    if command.lsp {
   226	        crate::lsp::run_lsp(external_linter, js_config_loader).await;
   227	        return CliRunResult::LintSucceeded;
   228	    }
   229	
   230	    init_miette();
   231	
   232	    command.handle_threads();
   233	
   234	    // stdio is blocked by LineWriter, use a BufWriter to reduce syscalls.
   235	    // See `https://github.com/rust-lang/rust/issues/60673`.
   236	    let mut stdout = BufWriter::new(std::io::stdout());
   237	
   238	    let mut cli_runner = CliRunner::new(command, external_linter);
   239	    #[cfg(feature = "napi")]
   240	    {
   241	        cli_runner = cli_runner.with_config_loader(js_config_loader);
   242	    }
   243	
   244	    cli_runner.run(&mut stdout)
   245	}
   246	
   247	#[cfg(all(target_pointer_width = "64", target_endian = "little"))]
   248	pub use crate::js_plugins::parse::{get_buffer_offset, parse_raw_sync};
   249	
   250	/// Returns `true` if raw transfer is supported on this platform.
   251	#[napi]
   252	pub fn raw_transfer_supported() -> bool {
   253	    cfg!(all(target_pointer_width = "64", target_endian = "little"))
   254	}

   110	        };

   112	        let mut override_builder = None;
   113	
   114	        if !ignore_options.no_ignore {
   115	            let mut builder = OverrideBuilder::new(&self.cwd);
   116	
   117	            if !ignore_options.ignore_pattern.is_empty() {
   118	                for pattern in &ignore_options.ignore_pattern {
   119	                    // Meaning of ignore pattern is reversed
   120	                    // <https://docs.rs/ignore/latest/ignore/overrides/struct.OverrideBuilder.html#method.add>
   121	                    let pattern = format!("!{pattern}");
   122	                    builder.add(&pattern).unwrap();
   123	                }
   124	            }
   125	
   126	            let builder = builder.build().unwrap();
   127	
   128	            // The ignore crate whitelists explicit paths, but priority
   129	            // should be given to the ignore file. Many users lint

   149	                    }

   363	        let report_unused_directives = if type_check_only {
   364	            None
   365	        } else {
   366	            match inline_config_options.report_unused_directives {
   367	                ReportUnusedDirectives::WithoutSeverity(true) => Some(AllowWarnDeny::Warn),
   368	                ReportUnusedDirectives::WithSeverity(Some(severity)) if severity.is_warn_deny() => {
   369	                    Some(severity)
   370	                }
   371	                ReportUnusedDirectives::WithSeverity(Some(_)) => None,
   372	                _ => match config_store.report_unused_disable_directives() {
   373	                    Some(severity) if severity.is_warn_deny() => Some(severity),
   374	                    _ => None,
   375	                },
   376	            }
   377	        };
   378	        let (mut diagnostic_service, tx_error) = Self::get_diagnostic_service(
   379	            &output_formatter,
   380	            &warning_options,
   381	            &misc_options,
   382	            max_warnings,
   383	        );
   384	
   385	        // Send JS plugins config to JS side
   386	        if let Some(external_linter) = &external_linter {
   387	            let res = config_store.external_plugin_store().setup_rule_configs(
   388	                self.cwd.to_string_lossy().into_owned(),
   389	                None,
   390	                external_linter,
   391	            );
   392	            if let Err(err) = res {
   393	                print_and_flush_stdout(
   394	                    stdout,
   395	                    &format!("Failed to setup JS plugin options:\n{err}\n"),
   396	                );
   397	                return CliRunResult::InvalidOptionConfig;
   398	            }
   399	        }
   400	
   401	        let files_to_lint = paths
   402	            .into_iter()
   403	            .filter(|path| !ignore_matcher.should_ignore(Path::new(path)))
   404	            .collect::<Vec<Arc<OsStr>>>();
   405	
   406	        let linter = Linter::new(LintOptions::default(), config_store, external_linter)
   407	            .with_fix(fix_options.fix_kind())
   408	            .with_report_unused_directives(report_unused_directives);
   409	
   410	        let number_of_files = files_to_lint.len();
   411	        let tsconfig = basic_options.tsconfig;
   412	        if let Some(path) = tsconfig.as_ref() {
   413	            if path.is_file() {
   414	                options = options.with_tsconfig(path);
   415	            } else {
   416	                let path = if path.is_relative() { options.cwd().join(path) } else { path.clone() };
   417	
   418	                print_and_flush_stdout(
   419	                    stdout,
   420	                    &format!(
   421	                        "The tsconfig file {:?} does not exist, Please provide a valid tsconfig file.\n",
   422	                        path.to_string_lossy().cow_replace('\\', "/")
   423	                    ),
   424	                );
   425	
   426	                return CliRunResult::InvalidOptionTsConfig;
   427	            }
   428	        }
   429	
   430	        let number_of_rules =
   431	            if type_check_only { None } else { linter.number_of_rules(type_aware) };
   432	
   433	        if number_of_files == 0 {
   434	            return Self::handle_no_files_found(
   435	                stdout,
   436	                &output_formatter,
   437	                now,
   438	                number_of_rules,
   439	                misc_options.no_error_on_unmatched_pattern,
   440	            );
   441	        }
   442	
   443	        // Create the LintRunner
   444	        // TODO: Add a warning message if `tsgolint` cannot be found, but type-aware rules are enabled
   445	        let lint_runner = match LintRunner::builder(options, linter)
   446	            .with_type_aware(type_aware)
   447	            .with_type_check(type_check)
   448	            .with_silent(misc_options.silent)
   449	            .with_fix_kind(fix_options.fix_kind())
   450	            .with_type_check_only(type_check_only)
   451	            .build()
   452	        {
   453	            Ok(runner) => runner,
   454	            Err(err) => {
   455	                print_and_flush_stdout(stdout, &err);
   456	                return CliRunResult::TsGoLintError;
   457	            }
   458	        };
   459	
   460	        match lint_runner.lint_files(&files_to_lint, tx_error.clone()) {
   461	            Ok(lint_runner) => {
   462	                lint_runner.report_unused_directives(report_unused_directives, &tx_error);
   463	            }
   464	            Err(err) => {
   465	                print_and_flush_stdout(stdout, &err);
   466	                return CliRunResult::TsGoLintError;
   467	            }
   468	        }
   469	
   470	        drop(tx_error);
   471	
   472	        let diagnostic_result = diagnostic_service.run(stdout);
   473	
   474	        if let Some(end) = output_formatter.lint_command_info(&LintCommandInfo {
   475	            number_of_files,
   476	            number_of_rules,
   477	            threads_count: rayon::current_num_threads(),
   478	            start_time: now.elapsed(),
   479	        }) {
   480	            print_and_flush_stdout(stdout, &end);
   481	        }
   482	
   483	        if diagnostic_result.errors_count() > 0 {
   484	            CliRunResult::LintFoundErrors
   485	        } else if deny_warnings && diagnostic_result.warnings_count() > 0 {
   486	            CliRunResult::LintNoWarningsAllowed
   487	        } else if diagnostic_result.max_warnings_exceeded() {
   488	            CliRunResult::LintMaxWarningsExceeded
   489	        } else {
   490	            CliRunResult::LintSucceeded
   491	        }
   492	    }
   493	}
   494	
   495	impl CliRunner {
   496	    #[must_use]
   497	    pub fn with_cwd(mut self, cwd: PathBuf) -> Self {
   498	        self.cwd = cwd;
   499	        self
   500	    }
   501	
   502	    #[cfg(feature = "napi")]
   503	    #[must_use]
   504	    pub fn with_config_loader(mut self, config_loader: Option<JsConfigLoaderCb>) -> Self {
   505	        self.js_config_loader = config_loader;
   506	        self
   507	    }
   508	
   509	    fn get_diagnostic_service(
   510	        reporter: &OutputFormatter,
   511	        warning_options: &WarningOptions,
   512	        misc_options: &MiscOptions,
   513	        max_warnings: Option<usize>,
   514	    ) -> (DiagnosticService, DiagnosticSender) {
   515	        let (service, sender) = DiagnosticService::new(reporter.get_diagnostic_reporter());
   516	        (
   517	            service
   518	                .with_quiet(warning_options.quiet)
   519	                .with_silent(misc_options.silent)
   520	                .with_max_warnings(max_warnings),
   521	            sender,
   522	        )
   523	    }
   524	
   525	    fn handle_no_files_found(
   526	        stdout: &mut dyn Write,
   527	        output_formatter: &OutputFormatter,
   528	        now: Instant,
   529	        number_of_rules: Option<usize>,
   530	        no_error_on_unmatched_pattern: bool,
   531	    ) -> CliRunResult {
   532	        if !no_error_on_unmatched_pattern {
   533	            print_and_flush_stdout(
   534	                stdout,
   535	                "No files found to lint. Please check your paths and ignore patterns.\n",
   536	            );
   537	        }
   538	
   539	        if let Some(end) = output_formatter.lint_command_info(&LintCommandInfo {
   540	            number_of_files: 0,
   541	            number_of_rules,
   542	            threads_count: rayon::current_num_threads(),
   543	            start_time: now.elapsed(),
   544	        }) {
   545	            print_and_flush_stdout(stdout, &end);
   546	        }
   547	
   548	        if no_error_on_unmatched_pattern {
   549	            CliRunResult::LintSucceeded
   550	        } else {
   551	            CliRunResult::LintNoFilesFound
   552	        }
   553	    }
   554	
   555	    // moved into a separate function for readability, but it's only ever used
   556	    // in one place.
   557	    fn get_filters(
   558	        filters_arg: Vec<(AllowWarnDeny, String)>,
   559	    ) -> Result<Vec<LintFilter>, (CliRunResult, String)> {
   560	        let mut filters = Vec::with_capacity(filters_arg.len());
   561	
   562	        for (severity, filter_arg) in filters_arg {
   563	            match LintFilter::new(severity, filter_arg) {
   564	                Ok(filter) => {
   565	                    filters.push(filter);
   566	                }
   567	                Err(InvalidFilterKind::Empty) => {
   568	                    return Err((
   569	                        CliRunResult::InvalidOptionSeverityWithoutFilter,
   570	                        format!("Cannot {severity} an empty filter.\n"),
   571	                    ));
   572	                }
   573	                Err(InvalidFilterKind::PluginMissing(filter)) => {
   574	                    return Err((
   575	                        CliRunResult::InvalidOptionSeverityWithoutPluginName,
   576	                        format!(
   577	                            "Failed to {severity} filter {filter}: Plugin name is missing. Expected <plugin>/<rule>\n"
   578	                        ),
   579	                    ));
   580	                }
   581	                Err(InvalidFilterKind::RuleMissing(filter)) => {
   582	                    return Err((
   583	                        CliRunResult::InvalidOptionSeverityWithoutRuleName,
   584	                        format!(
   585	                            "Failed to {severity} filter {filter}: Rule name is missing. Expected <plugin>/<rule>\n"
   586	                        ),
   587	                    ));
   588	                }
   589	            }
   590	        }
   591	
   592	        Ok(filters)
   593	    }
   594	}
   595	
   596	pub fn print_and_flush_stdout(stdout: &mut dyn Write, message: &str) {
   597	    stdout.write_all(message.as_bytes()).or_else(check_for_writer_error).unwrap();
   598	    stdout.flush().unwrap();
   599	}
   600	
   601	fn check_for_writer_error(error: std::io::Error) -> Result<(), std::io::Error> {
   602	    // Do not panic when the process is killed (e.g. piping into `less`).
   603	    if matches!(
   604	        error.kind(),
   605	        ErrorKind::Interrupted | ErrorKind::BrokenPipe | ErrorKind::WouldBlock
   606	    ) {
   607	        Ok(())
   608	    } else {
   609	        Err(error)
   610	    }
   611	}
   612	
   613	fn render_report(handler: &GraphicalReportHandler, diagnostic: &OxcDiagnostic) -> String {
   614	    let mut err = String::new();
   615	    handler.render_report(&mut err, diagnostic).unwrap();
   616	    err
   617	}
   618	
   619	fn render_config_builder_error(
   620	    handler: &GraphicalReportHandler,
